        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1486739411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14322174290808892436"><i>
  <b>“Magic will find those with pure hearts, <br/>even when all seems lost.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463180739i/19090716._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let me start by saying it's really hard for me to review books i love, there is so much i want to say.<br/>I know a lot people dislike these books so i decided to read a few bad reviews before i started this. Turned out most people had similar issues; too many characters, confusing plot line, too many POVs. <br/>I read first few chapters like a textbook, paid attention to every little detail, tried to remember their names, and who belo</span>
  <span id="freeText14322174290808892436" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“Magic will find those with pure hearts, <br>even when all seems lost.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463180739i/19090716._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me start by saying it's really hard for me to review books i love, there is so much i want to say.<br>I know a lot people dislike these books so i decided to read a few bad reviews before i started this. Turned out most people had similar issues; too many characters, confusing plot line, too many POVs. <br>I read first few chapters like a textbook, paid attention to every little detail, tried to remember their names, and who belonged where, once you get all that down this book is amazing! I love and hate all the characters. That's one of the things i loved about it that characters are more complex rather than just being pure evil or all goodness. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451873766i/17615545.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Then his heart, <br>now broken into a thousand pieces, <br>slowly began to turn to ice.”</i>
</b><br><br>^^(I fucking love this quote)<br><br><b>Magnus.</b><br>Magnus Lukas Damora, prince of blood, is a jackass. At first i felt sorry for him, he is obsessed with his sister and he feels disgusted with himself. I get it that he can't help it but things get really weird when he realizes she is not actually his sister. He has convinced himself whatever he is feeling is absolutely normal and there is nothing wrong with him. So he decides to go all psycho on her. Bad idea, buddy! At this point, i thought i had a pretty good idea what kind of character he was, but that changed when we saw him through Cleo's eyes. HE IS SO FREAKING SCARY AND CREEPY. He is a monster! I'm not sure i like him or not but i definitely enjoy reading about him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419036571i/12971931.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cleo.</b><br>Cleiona Aurora Bellos is the youngest princess of Auranos. Again, i didn't hate her but i didn't like her either but for totally different reasons. It's hard for me to connect with her. Many readers find her exasperating because she is spoiled, i didn't have that problem. Her older sister, the heir to the Auranian throne is dying and Cleo is seeking for magic that has been long forgotten to save her. She definitely grew on me by the end of the book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419036571i/12971932.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“If you want something, <br>you have to take it. <br>Because nobody's ever going to give it to you.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>Jonas.</b><br>Jonas is the youngest son of a wine-seller in Paelsia. After his older brother, Tomas gets killed cold-heartedly by one of Cleo's friend, Jonas seeks vengeance. He joins rebels to take over Paelsia. Now he fights for the freedom of his country against the tyranny of the King of Blood, King Gaius Damora. I. LOVED. HIM. Needless to say, he is my favorite of them all.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419036571i/12971933.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lucia.</b><br>Lucia Eva Damora, the prophesized sorceress. I feel really bad for her. First, she was taken away from her home when she was a baby. Her real mother was killed that night. She was brought up as a princess but the king and the queen never loved her. The king wants to use her powers and take over all kingdoms. The only person who she trusts is Magnus, her brother, who wants to sleep with her. On the surface she seems calm and polite but she's a ticking bomb, she is going to explode one day and fuck everything up. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442947085ra/16297102.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14322174290808892436" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1051308245" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1051308245" />
    <a title="Rachel E. Carter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29482005-rachel-e-carter"><img alt="Rachel E. Carter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512593159p2/29482005.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1051308245?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel E. Carter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel E. Carter" href="/user/show/29482005-rachel-e-carter">Rachel E. Carter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29482005-rachel-e-carter?shelf=br">br</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1051308245" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9981823234781658383"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462212820ra/18967557.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Do you like Game of Thrones and wish for a YA-version? Well, my friends, look no further:</i><br/><br/>•	Unexpected killings of significant characters?<br/>•	Multiple POV’s (including possible villains) taking place in different kingdoms with royalty, assassins, and other worldly creatures/shifters<br/>•	Heavy world-building<br/>•	Feuding kingdoms<br/>•	Even a brother-sister romance though that is a bit less Cersei-Jamie, a bit more Clary-Jace if you know what I mean=)<br/><br/>Is this book perfect? Well, honestly, I wasn’t a huge fan of </span>
  <span id="freeText9981823234781658383" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462212820ra/18967557.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Do you like Game of Thrones and wish for a YA-version? Well, my friends, look no further:</i><br><br>•	Unexpected killings of significant characters?<br>•	Multiple POV’s (including possible villains) taking place in different kingdoms with royalty, assassins, and other worldly creatures/shifters<br>•	Heavy world-building<br>•	Feuding kingdoms<br>•	Even a brother-sister romance though that is a bit less Cersei-Jamie, a bit more Clary-Jace if you know what I mean=)<br><br>Is this book perfect? Well, honestly, I wasn’t a huge fan of some of the main characters (blegh, Cleo), or the side characters (farmer boy), but there are other characters that make up for them: MAGNUS, MAGNUS, MAGNUS.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462212820ra/18967558.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I give you the cold-hearted prince that has the makings of a really hot, badass villain:<br><br><blockquote> “Then his heart, now broken into a thousand pieces, slowly began to turn to ice.”</blockquote><br><br>Magnus made the book for me. I need at least one character/romance to be invested in to enjoy a tale –no matter how exciting or kickass the characters may be- and he fulfilled that quota instantly. He’s dark, broody, sarcastic, untrusting, arrogant, aloof, dresses in all black and loves to drop sentences like this: <i>“Weak things are so easy to break”</i> &gt;&gt; ummm, well I may be a bit biased since he is basically Darren (from my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23365048.First_Year__The_Black_Mage___1_" title="First Year (The Black Mage, #1) by Rachel E. Carter" rel="nofollow noopener">First Year</a> series: <i>“Never trust a wolf, because the only thing the wolf will ever want to do is break you”</i> &gt;&gt; SEE WHAT I MEAN?). Clearly I have an affinity for badass, dark princes who have a weakness for only one thing and that is the girl they love… who also may accidentally turn him to the dark side if she betrays him… Oh snap, you didn’t hear me say that. I’m just saying, lots of coincidences to D-R which is fine by me ‘cause y’all know I love me some villainous princes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449249472ra/17256407.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But honestly Magnus was just part of the reason I loved this book. Falling Kingdoms was incredibly fast-paced, and while there was a lot of world-building, it didn’t have too many details to slow me down. The action was constant and there was never a boring chapter. I thought for a moment I would hate it after the incredibly fast build up to instalove between my two least favorite characters (Cleo &amp; her knight protector guy) but Morgan nipped that right in the bud and it was just badass the way she did it (never saw that coming!). There was so much action and drama and history that this book just flew by for me, and the crazy thing is when I finished I couldn’t believe I had only read one book –now I can’t wait to start the next (As well as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22571365.A_Book_of_Spirits_and_Thieves__Spirits_and_Thieves___1_" title="A Book of Spirits and Thieves (Spirits and Thieves, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">A Book of Spirits and Thieves</a> which I won at a book convention) because I want to know what happens. Just like Game of Thrones, this author is not promising us safety for any of the favorites –even a romance doesn’t save them! I can’t believe it took me so long to pick up this series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462212820ra/18967560.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9981823234781658383" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Anne by: </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=recommended-by-a-not-stupid-friend">recommended-by-a-not-stupid-friend</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475352100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16392836896297756924">3.5 stars<br/><br/>I had no idea this book even existed until my librarian gently pointed me toward this series. And by <i>gently</i>, I mean she flapped in front of my face, and told me it was a great series. And by <i>flapped it in front of my face</i>, I mean she threatened to revoke my (PRECIOUS!) card unless I read it.<br/><b>She's shady.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415034083ra/11718627.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So I check it out, and the next thing you know I'm all involved in a prince with incestuous thoughts, a princess being forced to marry a drunk, a young man from a poor village who dreams </span>
  <span id="freeText16392836896297756924" style="display:none">3.5 stars<br><br>I had no idea this book even existed until my librarian gently pointed me toward this series. And by <i>gently</i>, I mean she flapped in front of my face, and told me it was a great series. And by <i>flapped it in front of my face</i>, I mean she threatened to revoke my (PRECIOUS!) card unless I read it.<br><b>She's shady.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415034083ra/11718627.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So I check it out, and the next thing you know I'm all involved in a prince with incestuous thoughts, a princess being forced to marry a drunk, a young man from a poor village who dreams of revenge, a soon to be queen who is dying from a broken heart, a palace guard that may have fallen for his charge, a man masquerading as a hawk, and another princess who might have the power to restore the balance...or destroy the world.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428104410ra/14367897.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, and dead people. <br>Because every time you turn around somebody is getting shanked! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428103856ra/14367806.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think at least 3 people bit it in the prologue. You know, just to set the tone.<br>I'm guessing that's where the Game of Thrones references are coming from in all the other reviews. <br>Keep some booze handy, because nobody is safe in this sucker. <br>Nobody!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428105418ra/14368154.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Overall, this was really good, but with so many characters in play, it was hard to get a good flow going in the story. But that was really the only thing that kept this from being a solid 4 star read for me. With a little more momentum behind the plot, I think this bird will fly.<br>Now, I've been told by a reliable source (above mentioned crazy librarian) that this one gets better and better. And since she has the power to screw with all of my precious Pending Requests, I choose to believe her. In other words, I'll keep you guys updated on my progress with this series.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428106243ra/14368380.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><div>
  <a href="http://www.addicted2heroines.com/2015/04/review-falling-kingdoms-falling.html" title="Addicted 2 Heroines" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412937777i/11444542.jpg" alt="Addicted 2 Heroines" width="100%" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div></span>
  <a data-text-id="16392836896297756924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1555510711" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1555510711" />
    <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson"><img alt="Whitney Atkinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550868411p2/14457130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1555510711?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=unhauled">unhauled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=sent-from-pub">sent-from-pub</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1555510711" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1094084179251288205">Yay, now i'm only 18 books behind on my goodreads challenge, not 19.... :)<br/><br/>This book fell exactly where I expected it to, so 3 stars isn't a horrible rating! The main thing I loved about this is that it's different from any YA fantasy that i've ever read. The plot itself isn't really anything too special, but the scope of it all (following several characters/kingdoms instead of one main one) and the risks that the author is willing to take with characters (MANY deaths) kept me on my toes. The mai</span>
  <span id="freeText1094084179251288205" style="display:none">Yay, now i'm only 18 books behind on my goodreads challenge, not 19.... :)<br /><br />This book fell exactly where I expected it to, so 3 stars isn't a horrible rating! The main thing I loved about this is that it's different from any YA fantasy that i've ever read. The plot itself isn't really anything too special, but the scope of it all (following several characters/kingdoms instead of one main one) and the risks that the author is willing to take with characters (MANY deaths) kept me on my toes. The main downfall here was just how stupidly plain the writing was. I don't want to say that the author is talentless, but there were just some sentences I read that I could only go, "REALLY? That's the ONLY description you could come up with?" The descriptions are just so PLAIN I really couldn't put myself in any of the characters' shoes or get engrossed in the world. Literally, describing a character's hair color, the best she could come up with was "brownish." I know this may improve over the course of the next few books, but honestly I'm hesitating to continue them. My favorite character has a weird character arc going for him, and i'm not sure if it's worth it to get invested in these books if the only person I like dies. I own the next three, though, should I go for it? I feel very lukewarm about this and probably wouldn't regret it if I got rid of them, even though this one was entertaining for what it was worth.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1094084179251288205" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=reviewed-books">reviewed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=melting-inside-awwww">melting-inside-awwww</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=panic-attack">panic-attack</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sad-tragic-endings">sad-tragic-endings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer708359213" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17577320041334294037"><br/><b> RE-READ: SEP 2015<br/>Note - old review below but my thoughts have not changed....still loved it! </b> <br/><br/>****************************************************<br/><br/><b>“Even paradise could become a prison if one had enough time to take notice of the walls.</b>”<br/><br/>After seeing quite a few negative things about Falling Kingdoms on goodreads i was hesitant to buy it. But eventually i did, because, like, what the hell? Just cause some people disliked it doesn't mean that i will too! And i am so glad i did. <br/><br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/12/f4o.gif/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387308471ra/7574017.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://imageshack.us' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/>Why?<br/><br/>Because it w</span>
  <span id="freeText17577320041334294037" style="display:none"><br><b> RE-READ: SEP 2015<br>Note - old review below but my thoughts have not changed....still loved it! </b> <br><br>****************************************************<br><br><b>“Even paradise could become a prison if one had enough time to take notice of the walls.</b>”<br><br>After seeing quite a few negative things about Falling Kingdoms on goodreads i was hesitant to buy it. But eventually i did, because, like, what the hell? Just cause some people disliked it doesn't mean that i will too! And i am so glad i did. <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/12/f4o.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387308471ra/7574017.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>Why?<br><br>Because it was a total winner for me and i <b>LOVED</b> it!<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/594/9dv.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387308471ra/7574018.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/843/eyz.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387308471ra/7574019.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>FANS OF</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7896527.Throne_of_Glass__Throne_of_Glass___1_" title="Throne of Glass (Throne of Glass, #1) by Sarah J. Maas" rel="nofollow noopener">Throne of Glass</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496.A_Game_of_Thrones__A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire___1_" title="A Game of Thrones (A Song of Ice and Fire, #1) by George R.R. Martin" rel="nofollow noopener">A Game of Thrones</a> (both books and TV show) will <b>INHALE this outstanding high fantasy book </b>just like i did!<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/202/yvw.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387308471ra/7574020.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>
  <i>IN A LAND WHERE MAGIC HAS BEEN FORGOTTEN AND PEACE HAS REIGNED FOR CENTURIES, UNREST IS SIMMERING.<br><br>THREE KINGDOMS BATTLE FOR POWER.</i>
</b><br><br><b>A PRINCESS....</b><br> <br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/59/48z9.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387311018i/7574685.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Magic will find those with pure hearts, even when all seems lost.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>An Auranos princess must journey into enemy territory in search of a magic long thought extinct in order to safe her sister. But on her journey she will start the beginning of a new era.<br><br><b>A REBEL....</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/196/8hp9.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387311018i/7574686.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>A rebel with a heart made of ice will become the leader of a bloody revolution that will change everything. <br><br><b>A SORCERESS...</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/809/9qw5.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387311018i/7574687._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>A sorceress discovers the truth about the supernatural legacy she is destined to wield.<br><br><b>A SON OF A BLOOD KING.</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/577/5opn.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387317439i/7576006.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>Magnus is the son of the Limeros' cruel king (nicknamed the 'blood' king), and will either be a hero or the biggest villain Mystica will ever see. Will he surrender to the light?...Or to the dark?<br><br><b>
  <i>IT'S THE EVE OF WAR.<br>EACH MUST CHOOSE A SIDE.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>KINGDOMS <u>WILL</u> FALL.</i>
</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/163/5y3s.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387312570i/7575023.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>So you are probably confused, and trust me, i can see why. Let me clarify things for you, because i was really baffled at times in the beginning myself. <br><br>In the book the fantasy world is called <i>Mystica</i>, and is split up into 3 very different kingdoms. <br>1)<i>Auranos</i> - a beautiful, rich and 'happy' kingdom ruled by a fair king.<br>2) <i>Paelsia</i> - a starving, dusty, and harsh kingdom/place to live in, ruled by no one in particular. <br>3) <i>Limeros</i> - violent and disciplined kingdom ruled by the 'blood king'.<br><br><b>There are 4 protagonists and each play an essential part of the story. BUT there are a few more secondary characters POV's added to theirs. </b><br><br>You are probably all like this right now...<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/14/kyaq.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387317439i/7576007._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>I hope it makes a little sense at least, if not i promise you it will if you read the book!<br><br><b>
  <u>Characters: </u>
</b><br><b>Cloe</b><i>(princess)</i> - OMG. The majority of the book i thought she was a <b>spoiled little brat</b> who was <b>dumb</b> and very <b>naive</b>. <b>It seemed like EVERYONE was in love with her</b>. I felt like strangeling. She was exaggerating and acting like she was 5. Cloe was an immensely <b>ignorant</b> and <b>selfish</b> protagonist that i <b>had a hate/love relationship</b> towards the end. She did grow on me though, and at the end i thaught life has finally tought her a lesson and she grew up. Definitely became stronger. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You must draw from that strength. You must increase it. And you must hold on to it because sometimes that small glimmer of inner strength is all that we have to help us press forward through the darkness."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/571/hhd.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387317439ra/7576008.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>
  <u>Lucie and Magnus</u>
</b> i loved in the beginning.<b>NOT.ANYMORE</b>. After what they have done <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[to Auranos <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> i'm all like...<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/12/wfd.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387317439ra/7576009.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>There are many flaws in</b> <i>Falling kingdom</i> that make me understand why some readers disliked it. For example, the more than 1 love triangle and about million love interests. <br><br>But i <b>loved the fantasy world and the few legends</b>. I thought everything in this book was very interesting and i was intrigued throughout the book.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I have stories. But stories are not facts.'<br>'I like stories. Love them, actually. Most of the time they're better than facts.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>I was shocked a few times too</b>. Like when my favorite character died. I was like...<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/571/zok.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387384763ra/7587777.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>The end more than made up for the flaws, in my opinion.</b><br>It was so <b>emotional</b> it made me shed a tear or two! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The father scene at the end with Cleo... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/545/2a5.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387317439ra/7576010.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>
  <u>Overall</u>
</b>, Falling Kingdoms was a book that played with my feelings and took me on a <b>fantastic rollercoaster</b> i absolutely loved! It is <b>action-packed</b> and has a very <b>awesome plot</b> that i enjoyed. The cliffhanger at the end wasn't big but i still need book 2 ASAP (thank goodness it's out already!). <b>
  <u>Read this, guys</u>
</b>! :)<br><br><i>Sincerely - The Critic.</i><br><br> <br><b></b><br><u></u><br><i></i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Andreea Pop" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop"><img alt="Andreea Pop" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486663526p2/4858513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381587541?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andreea Pop" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andreea Pop" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop">Andreea Pop</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=annoying-heroine">annoying-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=never-again">never-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=wth-god-no">wth-god-no</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381587541" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9907271315841946781"><a href='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-23aZ7IyYQLE/VatcHl3YcuI/AAAAAAAAPRQ/gtxB4Jzn1Bk/s1600/tumblr_mfbanwGqOk1qejmu9o3_250.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565982.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I am truly sorry, I am. I wanted this book to be spectacular, to amaze me with its epicness. I was ready to love it heart and soul! Alas, sadly -- and very much obviously thanks to those two ugly stars -- that did not happen. I'm going to rant now, so please excuse my shouty capitals whenever they appear. <br/><br/>You see, my average rating is somewhere around 4.4/5 and seeing that I've read almost 500 titles that means I pretty much drop them 4 and 5 star ratings like they're hot. It doesn't bother </span>
  <span id="freeText9907271315841946781" style="display:none"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-23aZ7IyYQLE/VatcHl3YcuI/AAAAAAAAPRQ/gtxB4Jzn1Bk/s1600/tumblr_mfbanwGqOk1qejmu9o3_250.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565982.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am truly sorry, I am. I wanted this book to be spectacular, to amaze me with its epicness. I was ready to love it heart and soul! Alas, sadly -- and very much obviously thanks to those two ugly stars -- that did not happen. I'm going to rant now, so please excuse my shouty capitals whenever they appear. <br><br>You see, my average rating is somewhere around 4.4/5 and seeing that I've read almost 500 titles that means I pretty much drop them 4 and 5 star ratings like they're hot. It doesn't bother me, because I don't like wasting my time with books I know will bug me, so naturally that I'm choosing ones that will most likely suit me. Sometimes I miss and it results in the few and far between lower ratings. <br><br>But you know what all those good ratings of mine have in common? The answer is simple, folks: <b>characters</b>. You know, the ones that actually have a <i>character</i>. I don't care if there are 100 characters in a single story, give me <b>just one</b> that's not flat and I'll happily overlook the other 99 insipid ones for the sake of enjoyment. But when that one single "good" character fails to make its appearance, all hope is lost for me. A perfect example of that is <i>Falling Kingdoms</i>. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mKta8uwYAd0/VataXpB7ziI/AAAAAAAAPPo/blYGD6w5SqA/s1600/731425.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="167" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293448ra/15565906.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If there is one word I could use to describe the literary cast of this novel, it would be <b>weak</b>. Everyone is freaking dull, without a backbone and seriously <i>stupid</i>. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yYSK-IH2nTQ/VatcIP4uoSI/AAAAAAAAPRU/0skzMT3a6d4/s1600/tumblr_mr8jgpY4iW1se9fcoo1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="179" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565983.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There are 4 main POVs we have to endure and I honestly liked Jonas's the most, but the fact that he's practically the brightest in the bunch doesn't excuse his demeanor set on the mantra <i>hate royals, kill royals, get what the royals have.</i> <br><br>Now let me do you the honor of being acquainted with Princess Cleiona Bellos of Auranos, with a quote her highness herself offered. <br><br><blockquote>"He was her hero. He saved her once. He would save her again."</blockquote><br><br>She's the perfect <b>damsel in distress</b> and she's fucking okay with it. I hated her profoundly. If you thought Eadlyn from <i>The Heir</i> is a self-centered, selfish brat, you haven't met dear Cleo. Because even though she might not be exactly self-centered and selfish down to the core, she chooses to express her conflictual feelings internally, never doing anything to change facts, never taking a stand, happily obliging to choke down her worries. And that's somehow worse. She's also plain childish and immature. 16 years old? More like 8. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-J-uUqFcljBc/VatcEtN16CI/AAAAAAAAPQw/sDln1RoLC_I/s1600/10222359.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="165" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565984.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let's get on to Magnus, who's apparently <i>a dark and tormented prince</i>. Truly, <b>he's not</b>. He's much more of an emo coward with the impression of being powerful. I'm not gonna lie, he's messed up in the head and even my boundless love for tall, dark, handsome princelings couldn't make him appealing in my eyes. Besides the fact that he's obsessed with his sister -- <b>ew ew ew</b> -- he doesn't have much of a personality. I'll say that he has the potential for a strange, mysterious hero, but it has never come to fruition in this first installment.<br><br>Lucia, Magnus's said-sister, is really adopted -- but still ew ew -- and also the possible sorceress the stars prophesied about that has immense power. She was such a pitiful puppet in this book and, for the love of God, try as I might I still couldn't connect with her. We know she's beautiful, that she loves her brother, that she has countless suitors and that she can do magic. And that's all. No development, no real insight into her personal traits. <b>NOTHING.</b> <br><br>The secondary characters were laughable. We have the basic clichés of elder and wise sibling, the best friend who's in love with the girl and the father who's spoiled his child to no end. Chief Basilius was an idiot. King Gaius reminded me of the King of Erilea but he was nowhere near his capacity of portraying a good villain. Don't get me started on Aron because that shit with eyes could've saved me the pain of this book if he hadn't wanted to get drunk on the best wine ever.<br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-aRKO2kVxH0I/VatcEsgzuwI/AAAAAAAAPQ4/STioMpZP1Vo/s1600/anigif_f85a43ee7578fbb7832864c769eed7ce-4.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="172" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565985.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I won't even bother explaining the plotline, because from the get-go it had such a bad foundation I can't even tell you. Sure, there were a few fantasy elements that probably saved me from giving this one a 1 star rating (magic, prophecies and some watchers), but besides that? Only predictable and boring outcomes. <br><br>Seriously though: <br>WHAT KIND OF ROYALTY THINKS IT'S OKAY TO VENTURE INTO THE UNKNOWN WITHOUT A GUARD?! <br><br>WHAT KIND OF LEADER DOESN'T CONCERN HIMSELF WITH THE FACT THAT HIS NEW-FOUND ALLY MIGHT ACTUALLY SCREW HIM OVER?! <br><br>WHAT KIND OF A SUPPOSEDLY TRAINED GUARD KILLS TWO SOLDIERS, MAKES GOOGLY EYES AT GIRL FOR ETERNITY AND THEN GETS HIMSELF KILLED BY FORGETTING ABOUT A THIRD DUDE?! <br><br>Arghhhh. Oh, and let's not forget about a certain someone not knowing something incredibly important is right in her grasp until of course it's too late. <br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UotbWw_0o60/VatcFPcJE0I/AAAAAAAAPQ8/9Js-eEFSAxg/s1600/kjb.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565986.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There were two ounces of romance in this one and none was a winner. Firstly, we have Cleo and Theon's forbidden "love" that had the quality of being also insta-love since although time passes between their interactions, we don't get to see anything of that. One sec we're meeting them both and then, after a few chapters with multiple POV swaps, we're supposed to believe they developed feelings? I don't believe it till I see it, so <b>NOPE</b> from me. Secondly, we have Magnus and Lucia and the girl has brains for pushing him away, I'll give her that, because I know they're not related but for 16 long years they were <b>RAISED</b> as they were so anything beyond a deep friendship and brotherly love (like in Lucia's part) shouldn't even exist. Again, ew ew ew. <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gl_vxInCB_I/Vatc_ApNXFI/AAAAAAAAPRk/zW0e0sOuf7Q/s1600/30398db530680d6608f65e2852797351.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="156" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565987.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh, I almost forgot the cherry on the top! The <i>fantastical</i> world-building! This continent, called Mytica, that has only three states (Limeros, Paelsia and Auranos) and that could probably be travelled from one corner to the other in less than a week. Oh, please. They're talking about world-domination and their land is the size of a small island!<br><br>I really really need to talk a bit about the ending because I was almost happy dancing the book was over and then it punched me again with Cleo's stupidity. As if I needed a reminder. With the price of being <b>spoilery</b> (no worries, you would have figured it out yourself nonetheless if you actually read the book), I am going to ask: <b>Who the fuck doesn't flee his newly-conquered kingdom and sits in the fucking courtyard listening to a fucking speech when you're the goddamned wanted princess?!?</b> <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GvcUt6dN0SM/VatcEmaLJRI/AAAAAAAAPQ0/3rZJsEoxhFc/s1600/Who-GIF.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="177" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437293964ra/15565988.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh, that's right. Cleiona <i>fucking</i> Bellos. Kill me now, please. <br><br>Also, the cover? With that badass looking killer and daggers and mysterious cloak? Totally not having anything to do with the book besides the mere appearance of that tiny hawk. <br><br>To sum up, I didn't downright hated <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> (IKR, it's hard to believe), because after all I did finish it and I might even entertain the incredulous idea of picking up its sequel -- if I'm very very bored or I lack a piece of good literature at the moment. But I sure as hell wouldn't recommend it, because, in the end, I don't care what happens to these characters now and that is always problematic if you want to read something memorable. <br><br><b>ENJOY! &lt;3 </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9907271315841946781" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1700747307" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16204069163293892315">This was one of those books that didn't seem to want to go forward. It dragged especially the first half and then dragged some more. <br/><br/><a href='http://67.media.tumblr.com/d1a620a328a94ee78f8169607bd70b38/tumblr_nx9azvRI5v1txpkowo1_500.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479722743ra/21226316.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>There was potential, sure but all shattered when it was clear that everything and i mean EVERYTHING needs to be <b>discussed to death.</b> I only wish it was literally <i>to their deaths</i> so I didn't have to continue with them anymore. <br/><br/>Really. So fucking tedious.<br/><br/>Give me the story. <br/>Do something. <br/>Anything! <br/><br/>Cleo, you wanna go <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[to Paelsia? <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Go the</span>
  <span id="freeText16204069163293892315" style="display:none">This was one of those books that didn't seem to want to go forward. It dragged especially the first half and then dragged some more. <br><br><a href="http://67.media.tumblr.com/d1a620a328a94ee78f8169607bd70b38/tumblr_nx9azvRI5v1txpkowo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479722743ra/21226316.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There was potential, sure but all shattered when it was clear that everything and i mean EVERYTHING needs to be <b>discussed to death.</b> I only wish it was literally <i>to their deaths</i> so I didn't have to continue with them anymore. <br><br>Really. So fucking tedious.<br><br>Give me the story. <br>Do something. <br>Anything! <br><br>Cleo, you wanna go <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[to Paelsia? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Go then. Go or stay i don't care! Just fricking do it already! I can't read anymore of your discussions about this same tiresome subject - i've read three, <i>three</i> goddamn talks about this! And they lasted pages! Come the F on!<br><br><br>This thing had way too many POVs and none of them particularly well done.<br><br><br><s>Dnf@79%<br><i>*marked as dnf for now*</i></s><br><br><br>Wouldn't you believed it? <br>I actually went back and <b>finished</b> this!<br>I know shocking! BUT I've <i>heard</i> this was the weakest book in the series. So I figured 'finish it and have an option to move on to book 2 if the mood strikes'<br><br>The rating remains the same for this book though.<br><br><a href="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480287522ra/21293276.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480287522ra/21293276.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1815514184" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1815514184" />
    <a title="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen"><img alt="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560356189p2/47627265.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1815514184?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" href="/user/show/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen">Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=why-the-hype">why-the-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1815514184" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4601310949860152756"><b> 2 Stars<br/><br/>Overview: </b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486496557ra/21920799.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series is often hailed the ‘<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496.A_Game_of_Thrones__A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire___1_' title='A Game of Thrones (A Song of Ice and Fire, #1) by George R.R. Martin' rel='nofollow noopener'>Game of Thrones</a> for YA' and because I haven’t read/watched GOT, I can’t comment on the comparison. <br/><br/>I <i>can</i> tell you the similarities. They're both fantasy series involving a large cast of characters, murder, magic, and backstabbing. <s>Also incest!</s> Here, however, the overarching story focuses on the intersecting lives of Cleo, Jonas, and Magnus as war blossoms between their nations. <br/><br/><b> Pros: </b><br/><br/>There were several deaths I didn’t expect! Most didn't feel </span>
  <span id="freeText4601310949860152756" style="display:none"><b> 2 Stars<br><br>Overview: </b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486496557ra/21920799.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series is often hailed the ‘<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13496.A_Game_of_Thrones__A_Song_of_Ice_and_Fire___1_" title="A Game of Thrones (A Song of Ice and Fire, #1) by George R.R. Martin" rel="nofollow noopener">Game of Thrones</a> for YA' and because I haven’t read/watched GOT, I can’t comment on the comparison. <br><br>I <i>can</i> tell you the similarities. They're both fantasy series involving a large cast of characters, murder, magic, and backstabbing. <s>Also incest!</s> Here, however, the overarching story focuses on the intersecting lives of Cleo, Jonas, and Magnus as war blossoms between their nations. <br><br><b> Pros: </b><br><br>There were several deaths I didn’t expect! Most didn't feel senseless and still pushed the story forward, while also adding a threat of danger that made everything more exciting. <br><br>The history of the three-lands and their opposing views of the same goddesses was very interesting to me. In fact, most of the mythology in this was intriguing and I wish it had been expanded upon.<br><br>I thought several characters have potential. I actually liked Cleo? She was definitely a little spoiled, but I could already see improvement. I really liked Lucia and Nic as well. Lucia’s story is arguably the most interesting, and I appreciated how well she stood up for herself/loved ones. <br><br>None of the characters are 100% morally good and some teetered anti-hero territory. This wasn't carried out well, but it was something I appreciated. <br><br><b> Cons </b><br><br>Why did Alexius only have like three chapters? Why were they only 2 pages long? Why was his POV even there if it didn't impact the story at all?? <br><br>I never really connected with any of the characters. I understand their motivations and how I’m <i>supposed</i> to feel—but mainly because Rhodes reiterated it 50 times. For example:<br><br>	<i>
  <blockquote> “I hate them. I’d kill them all for a chance of a life like their's.” </blockquote>
</i><br><i>
  <blockquote>"He had spent time in her bed, listened to her gossip about her friends, to her stories about her hateful snakes, all in an attempt to gain the chief’s confidence so that he might convince him to rise up against the Auranians and take what should have been theirs.” </blockquote>
</i><br><br><br>Everyone’s motivation is <i>explicitly</i> stated. There's no guesswork or showing anything through actions. It was boring and made even worse when motivation would <i>rapidly</i> change. A character went from soley seeking revenge to clamoring for war, then a few chapters later he was advocating for peace. <br><br>And somehow everything is so <i>convenient?</i> Jonas is able to talk freely with the leader of his country, the first person Cleo interacts with in a new country is able to give her the information she wants, everyone is blinded by Cleo’s beauty, apologies are made and accepted through the aid of cute rabbits, etc. Quite a lot was just unbelievable occurrences pushing the plot forward. <br><br>Prologue was completely unnecessary and gave away what could have been a cool plot-twist. <br><br>The writing itself wasn’t great. <s>Sorry, not sorry.</s> And I've listed my three biggest problems with it.<br><br>1.	There was <i>a lot</i> of stitled dialogue:<br>	<i>
  <blockquote>“Paelisan scum,” he snarled as he raised his sword “Die you maggot!”</blockquote>
</i><br>	<i>
  <blockquote> “Tell my mother I love her. And that I did this for her.” </blockquote>
</i><br>	<i>
  <blockquote> “The princess isn’t in her room. She’s nowhere to be found!” </blockquote>
</i> <br><br>2.	Repeated wording. Certain phrases were consistently reused every few chapters:<br><br><i>"A muscle under Sabina’s right eye twitched, almost imperceptibly."</i> Then a few chapters later, <i>“A muscle in Brion’s cheek twitched.” </i> <br><br>3.	Clunky sentences with a lot of filler words. Take below for an example, did we really need so many ‘that’s and ‘had’s??<br><br><i>
  <blockquote> “I had no idea that the difficulties between the lands would result in conflict like this. I spoke with King Gaius, who told me that he had [spoiler].” </blockquote>
</i><br><br>It was never horrible, it just wasn’t great. <br><br><b> In Conclusion </b><br><br>Oddly, I <i>really</i> enjoyed reading this! No doubt because this was a Buddy Read with these awesome people in a fun fantasy league: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7971097" rel="nofollow noopener">Bentley</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829" rel="nofollow noopener">Mary</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/61971658-frankie-lovely" rel="nofollow noopener">Frankie</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17441031" rel="nofollow noopener">Jeremy</a>, and<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26462337" rel="nofollow noopener"> Rachelle</a>. &lt;3 <br><br>They are all awesome, and their commentary made the whole thing worth it!<br><br>Taking a little break before we move on to the second book, and I saw potential here, so maybe it’ll be better?</span>
  <a data-text-id="4601310949860152756" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText2136444389605750509" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Ouuu, I liked this book....despite a few things. </i>
</b><br /><br />RTC...<i>When I'm not: </i><br /><br /><b>1) Lazy as fuck<br />2) SCHOOL <br />3) SCHOOL<br />4) LIFE<br />5) Yup, lazy as fuck again ;P</b><br /><br />Anyway, gimme the next book pls!<br /><br />**************************<br /><br />I went to the library to <b> ACTUALLY </b> study and do my school work. Okay, I'm trying make it to places GUYS !! <b> *cough* </b>I should've thought about becoming a Doctor like <i>holyyyyyyyy shit. The work load ISN'T A JOKEEEE. </i><br /><br />Please tell me how I walk inside and the first thing I see is a big ass book sale. Everything was being sold for $1.....<br /><br /><b>YOU SEE THAT ?? <br /><br />ALL<br /><br />FOR <br /><br />$1 </b><br /><br />My inner self and I have accepted that we can't escape books. Of all days, I wanted to be a good ass student, get all my work done and <b>BAMMM!!</b> The book Life hits me like a damn Train ಥ_ಥ<br /><br />I was going to close my eyes and sprint right by the book sale section because <b> *cough* </b> I'm broke af. Luckily, I remembered I made sure to take some money from my mom because there's a really <i> bigggggggg </i> Starbucks near the library. And yeah, Tweebs wants her Starbucks. They have this really nice drink my friend forced me to try that legit tastes like it came straight out of heaven. If you have a Starbucks nearby then I'd advise you to please get the <b> "Caramel Frappe" </b> <br /><br />YOU'LL THANK MEEEEE GUYS =) !!<br /><br />Anyway, as I was getting ready to sprint; <i> I swear, </i> this lady, who was selling the books, was looking into my soul like <b>"I know you're a book addict. It's written all over you. I bet a million dollars, you got zero guts to actually walk by and not buy some books. Best deals like you be missing out on this beautiful opportunity. I double D dare your ass to continue walking.<i><br /><br />Comeeeeeee<br /><br />hereeeeeee.<br /><br />youuuu<br /><br />littleeeee<br /><br />shittttt<br /><br />headdddd </i>" </b><br /><br /><i>SOOOOO yeah, </i> I bought 4 books. I stopped myself from going crazy because I didn't want to return home with 3849384392 books. Not that I could because <b>I'M ACTUALLY REPRESENTING TEAM BROKE. </b>I have to get a job guys like for real....<b><br /><br />SOMEONE HIRE MY ASS LIKE HOW COULD ANYONE NOT WANT SUCH AN AMAZING, CUTE, FUNNY, SASSY, SAVAGE, YEAH...the list of qualities is endless</b><br /><br /> <br />Didn't know I'd make this pre-review this long but what can I say?? I got carried away. All I wanted to say is....Don't let me down because I heard a lot about you, <i> Oh Falling Kingdom One </i> :) :) :) :)</span>

<div id="review_2167014932" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2167014932" />
    <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52207144"><img alt="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568965358p2/52207144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2167014932?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" href="/user/show/52207144">♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/20320771-falling-kingdoms">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=dystopia-and-utopian">dystopia-and-utopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=2018-reading-challenge">2018-reading-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2167014932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8736729438785267076"><u>4 Princess. Rebel. Sorceress. Hire. ★'s</u> <br/><br/><i>“You must continue to believe with all your heart. Sometimes belief is all it takes to make something real.”</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>'Falling Kingdoms' was so good! I was hooked from the first page and I finished it in one sitting. I couldn't put this book down, it drew me right in and it was also a fast passed read. I enjoyed the plot, the writing style was captivating, the world was enchanting and well thought out. As were the characters, the character building was done nicely a</span>
  <span id="freeText8736729438785267076" style="display:none"><u>4 Princess. Rebel. Sorceress. Hire. ★'s</u> <br><br><i>“You must continue to believe with all your heart. Sometimes belief is all it takes to make something real.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>'Falling Kingdoms' was so good! I was hooked from the first page and I finished it in one sitting. I couldn't put this book down, it drew me right in and it was also a fast passed read. I enjoyed the plot, the writing style was captivating, the world was enchanting and well thought out. As were the characters, the character building was done nicely and they were all very enjoyable. I loved getting to know each and everyone of them and learning about the different kingdoms. I really enjoyed all the back stories too. The best part though was all the different characters and the different lives that they lead. They were all enticing, had depth and lots of room for growth. Truly it's so hard to choose a favorite. But... I do really love Princess Cleo, then again I really love all four of the main characters. I also love how none of the character are all good or all bad. The choices they make determines the paths in-witch they travel and some of those choices are leading them down some pretty dark alleys :( But every story needs a good villain or two in this case. The Kingdoms are fighting for <b>POWER</b> and in its wake, is so much blood, destruction, betrayal, and chaos. Sadly, so many die in this first book and one in particular completely shocked me!!! I was so <b>NOT</b> expecting that character to die so soon. But war is war, and I have a feeling that many, many, more will die before it's all said and done! There are so many twists and turns, and surprises at every corner. I love reading books with multiple POVs and this book has many :D <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> is sure to draw you in and break your heart. It broke mine, and it also had me tearing up in a few places. It gave me all kinds of feels! Everything felt really planned out and it was addicting. I believe, I have found my new addiction and I can't wait to see what adventures await me in Rebel Spring book #2. <br><br><b>*I love this cover a lot!*</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Hate is such a strong emotion. Much more powerful than indifference. But those who burn with hate can also love just as intensely. Can't they? When you hate--or love--do you do so with all your heart? So much that it feels as if you might die from it?”</i><br><br><i>“Even in the darkest and most cruel person, there is still a kernel of good. And within the most perfect champion, there is darkness. The question is, will one give in to the dark or the light? It's something we decide with every choice we make, every day that we exist. What might not be evil to you could be evil to someone else. Knowing this makes us powerful even without magic.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I’ll be strong,” she whispered. “I’ll be strong for you. For Emilia. For Theon. For Auranos. I swear I’ll make them pay for what they’ve done.”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522711283ra/25313880.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“In any case, her fight was not over yet—not nearly over. It had only begun. And yes, Cleo would be strong. Just as her father and Emilia had asked her to be. She would be strong. She would reclaim her rightful throne. She would be queen.”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8736729438785267076" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3660854006501169871">*unmarked spoilers ahead, read at your own risk. *<br/><br/><b> buddy read with </b> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3283298-jessica' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jessica, fellow Theon lover.</a> 🍦<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1521148260ra/25219572.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh, wow. I did <i> not </i> expect this to become a 5 star read for me, but it really did. I got so emotionally invested in every single character, which I never expected!<br/><br/>Firstly, I need to put it out there that this was like And I Darken/Now I Rise+fantasy+magic= amazing. I was getting so many feels for the Conqueror's Saga, my utmost favorite series. I LOVED IT 😻😻<br/><br/>The world building, the magic, the charac</span>
  <span id="freeText3660854006501169871" style="display:none">*unmarked spoilers ahead, read at your own risk. *<br><br><b> buddy read with </b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3283298-jessica" rel="nofollow noopener">Jessica, fellow Theon lover.</a> 🍦<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1521148260ra/25219572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, wow. I did <i> not </i> expect this to become a 5 star read for me, but it really did. I got so emotionally invested in every single character, which I never expected!<br><br>Firstly, I need to put it out there that this was like And I Darken/Now I Rise+fantasy+magic= amazing. I was getting so many feels for the Conqueror's Saga, my utmost favorite series. I LOVED IT 😻😻<br><br>The world building, the magic, the characters, I loved it all and hated all the snakes that were slithering around everywhere (cough cough Sabina) &amp; I am just so happy I read this book! It's one of those series that everyone raves about and you can't wait to board the hype train. <br><br>Definitely plot and character driven, so I'll give my thoughts on both: <br><br><b> Cleo </b>: so first, I thought I wasn’t going to like her because she just stood by, doing nothing, making naive decisions. But she PULLED HERSELF TOGETHER &amp; I really loved her near the end. I can’t wait to see what the next books hold for her &amp; her stubborn witty personality!<br><br><b> Magnus </b> : alright so I thought I wasn’t going to like him AT ALL. but whenever he was sad I felt my heart sink for him &amp; I felt so bad for him. Like please let me give you all the love you deserve? shoot, I think I just admitted that I like him. but he’s still an arrogant and rude and evil ass. what a mess. <br><br><b> Theon </b> : I’m tearing up. I started to love him 5% through the book and him and Cleo were beautiful? Like give me more? Oh no, but Morgan Rhodes just had to kill him off. It’s fine. I’m fine. How am I supposed to get through with this? How? How will I ever forgive Magnus? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1521148260ra/25219571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Boy, was I glad to see Sabina burn. King Corvin was the best &amp; I’m still not over his death. He just took so much care of his daughters and loved them unlike Gaius who uses his children. MAGNUS BACK AWAY AND RUN AND HIDE. Also, what in the world was the Chief he made me so mad &amp; annoyed like get out and take your topless dancing girls with you, sir. <br>Lucia was also pretty annoying. Jonas was okay, I guess, warmed up to him a bit but good luck marrying the dancing snake lady. Also, I'm done with Nic. Also I miss you Emilia. &amp; Simon, even though I didn’t know him. This comes to show how much effect the characters had on me. Even Tomas, who I didn’t even know for a page. I’m so sorry. AND ARON, oh ARON was the worst. <br><br>okay my feelings are all messed up seriously, can you even call this a review because it really is jut all my feelings written out in an extremely incoherent way. but read THIS BOOK and I need the next and all the books and the series in general because this is fantasy. This. Is. Fantasy. <br><br>I’m so embarrassed to have written this review I promise I’m not like this all the time. <br><br></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21530568-rusty-s-ghost-engine-also-known-as-jinky-spring?shelf=this-is-fucking-awesome">this-is-fucking-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21530568-rusty-s-ghost-engine-also-known-as-jinky-spring?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer927055756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13280923951689336793">Blog review <a href='https://edwardsghostengine.wordpress.com/2017/09/06/falling-kingdoms-morgan-rhodes/' rel='nofollow noopener'>@Scaredy Engines End of Line Library</a><br/><br/>There is a lot of drama and plot twists in this book. A lot. Which is what made it so enjoyable for me! :D <br/><br/>First of all the characters and world were so richly developed I could not guess what was around the next corner. Like I've said in other reviews one of the most enjoyable aspects of a high fantasy novel is the world building and Myticas history was full of intrigue not to mention how I loved the stories from the past catching up and intertwin</span>
  <span id="freeText13280923951689336793" style="display:none">Blog review <a href="https://edwardsghostengine.wordpress.com/2017/09/06/falling-kingdoms-morgan-rhodes/" rel="nofollow noopener">@Scaredy Engines End of Line Library</a><br /><br />There is a lot of drama and plot twists in this book. A lot. Which is what made it so enjoyable for me! :D <br /><br />First of all the characters and world were so richly developed I could not guess what was around the next corner. Like I've said in other reviews one of the most enjoyable aspects of a high fantasy novel is the world building and Myticas history was full of intrigue not to mention how I loved the stories from the past catching up and intertwining with the characters of present. In a way it felt like everything was explained at the end of the book regarding the intentions of the characters and the magic at stake, but with definite room for more adventures and more problems to solve. (This is an ongoing series after all)<br /><br />I liked how the author managed to create a believable world and fill it with complex characters whose intentions aren't always clear at least not until the end. In fact the characters were so well written that their feelings and actions felt real to me. Cleo was a character I didn't like at the beginning but I feel she really grew out of that spoiled princess cast and came to realise there was a lot at stake. That cliffhanger ending with her definitely makes me want to grab the next book ASAP. <br /><br />On my copy there is a statement which says "perfect for fans of game of thrones ". I cannot comment on this as I have never read the book or seen the tv series. But I have a general idea as to what game of thrones is about and based on that idea I would say that statement is right. Highly recommended</span>
  <a data-text-id="13280923951689336793" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xYeD042+7NstkbrT2JC4YtmSkL+YTi92qJcHnR80Sic/grYuAAncOD/0PnL1zqVF6jfYppWJXlm7dxsAbDbtrQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vpeoXZQTA0ImzJnRPXzURO5Buacxo+JX+TnNS4zmCa1Ekp2gGaQzoTSpHXAQIslj3eTxvjxkk3jq2dHW/+SuJw==')})
  }
//]]>

They\'re <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText7585939507290413455\" style=\"display:none\">Times are hard in the mountain city of Fellsmarch. Reformed thief Han Alister will do almost anything to eke out a living for his family. The only thing of value he has is something he can\'t sell—the thick silver cuffs he\'s worn since birth. They\'re clearly magicked—as he grows, they grow, and he\'s never been able to get them off.\n\nOne day, Han and his clan friend, Dancer, confront three young wizards setting fire to the sacred mountain of Hanalea. Han takes an amulet from Micah Bayar, son of the High Wizard, to keep him from using it against them. Soon Han learns that the amulet has an evil history—it once belonged to the Demon King, the wizard who nearly destroyed the world a millennium ago. With a magical piece that powerful at stake, Han knows that the Bayars will stop at nothing to get it back.\n\nMeanwhile, Raisa ana\'Marianna, princess heir of the Fells, has her own battles to fight. She\'s just returned to court after three years of freedom in the mountains—riding, hunting, and working the famous clan markets. Raisa wants to be more than an ornament in a glittering cage. She aspires to be like Hanalea—the legendary warrior queen who killed the Demon King and saved the world. But her mother has other plans for her...\n\nThe Seven Realms tremble when the lives of Hans and Raisa collide, fanning the flames of the smoldering war between clans and wizards.<\/span>\n  <a <span id="freeTextContainer5942597466749051414">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet vor</span>
  <span id="freeText5942597466749051414" style="display:none">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet voracious reader of all kinds of books. Under another pen name, she’s a national bestselling author of many paranormal novels. Falling Kingdoms is her first high fantasy. </span>
